	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/OIDplusMailUtils.class.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusMailUtils.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusMailUtils.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusMailUtils.class.php') != 'cc41dc225c5bd9e96906ba2a4abf7529b75bfdc1') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusMailUtils.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusMailUtils.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusMailUtils.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusMailUtils.class.php') !== 'cc41dc225c5bd9e96906ba2a4abf7529b75bfdc1') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusMailUtils.class.php') !== '8807824bf24c7c5f3766112e8d79a2bf68736c89') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusMailUtils.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplusMailUtils.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplusMailUtils.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusMailUtils.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusMailUtils.class.php') !== 'cc41dc225c5bd9e96906ba2a4abf7529b75bfdc1') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusMailUtils.class.php');
		}
	}

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'eea2461bf15ed2aae5eb02c1c912891f9abaa5d3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'eea2461bf15ed2aae5eb02c1c912891f9abaa5d3') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'adb5ec3037fc1f41b1cca45269c0d2868d875ca5') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'eea2461bf15ed2aae5eb02c1c912891f9abaa5d3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}
